CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "cars_car" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "name" varchar(100) NOT NULL, "slug" varchar(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE, "seats" varchar(10) NOT NULL, "year" integer NOT NULL, "price_min" integer NULL, "price_max" integer NULL, "brand_id" bigint NOT NULL REFERENCES "cars_brand" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "performance_id" bigint NULL UNIQUE REFERENCES "cars_performance" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "cars_engine" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "cylinder_layout" varchar(1) NULL, "cylinder_count" smallint unsigned NULL CHECK ("cylinder_count" >= 0), "aspiration" varchar(1) NULL, "engine_capacity" integer unsigned NULL CHECK ("engine_capacity" >= 0), "battery_capacity" real NULL, "horsepower" integer unsigned NULL CHECK ("horsepower" >= 0), "torque" integer unsigned NULL CHECK ("torque" >= 0), "car_id" bigint NOT NULL REFERENCES "cars_car" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
